STRAX™ API documentation version v2

http://{environment}.strax.co

  • environment: required (string)

    Name of the environment

STRAX™ Login API

/api/login post

post

API to authenticate / let users login into STRAX. Same as /api/participants/doAuthenticate

post /api/login

API to authenticate / let users login into STRAX. Same as /api/participants/doAuthenticate

  • Request
  • Response

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • username: required (string - minLength: 3 - maxLength: 100 - pattern: [A-Z0-9a-z._+-@]*)

    Valid email address provided by the agency

    Example:

    user@example.com
  • password: required (string)

    Example:

    str*ngPa55w*rd
  • fingerprint: (string)

    A uniqe identifier for the device used to sign-in

  • fpData: (array of )

    List of parameters used to compute fingerprint

  • applnType: required (one of Web Application, Android Application, iOS Application)

    Type of application the user is logging in from

  • applnName: required (one of STRAX APP AngularJS, STRAX APP VueJS, STRAX Mobile Android)

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • appTicket: required (object)

    Application ticket used to request Auth ticket from ID Server. It contains the app-id and scope.

    • firstName: required (string)
    • lastName: required (string)
    • partId: required (string)
    • role: required (string)

      As of now, role determines whether the user is a viewer, user, controller or EEI Support

    • rsvp: required (string)

      A string with grant associated to retrieve auth ticket from the ID server.

    • token: required (string)

      JWT token used to embed details required by the the UI

    • vertical: (string)

      LOB "eagleeye"

    HTTP status code 401

    Invalid Credentials

    Body

    Media type: application/json

    Type: object

    Properties
    • code: required (string)
    • message: required (string)

    Example:

    {
  "code": "STRLGN001",
  "message": "Invalid Credentials"
}

    HTTP status code 500

    Body

    Media type: application/json

    Type: object

    Properties
    • code: required (string)
    • message: required (string)

    Example:

    {
  "code": "STRLGN004",
  "message": "Unable to login. System Error."
}

    Account Management

    A collection of Accounts

    /api/accounts get post

    get

    Get all Account records data

    post

    Create a new Account record

    get /api/accounts

    Get all Account records data

    Secured by oz_ticket
    • Request
    • Response
    • Security

    Query Parameters

    • name: (string)
    • mnemonic: (string)

    HTTP status code 200

    Body

    Media type: application/json

    Type: array of Accounts

    Items: Accounts

    • _id: (object)
      • accountNumber: required (string)
      • accountName: required (string - maxLength: 100)
      • address: required (object)
        • formattedAddress: (string - maxLength: 200)
        • geo: (any)
        • additionalInfo: (any)
      • phone: required (string)
      • website: required (string - maxLength: 50)
      • mnemonic: (string - minLength: 2 - maxLength: 20 - pattern: [A-Z])

      Secured by oz_ticket

      Headers

      • Authorization: required (string)

        Used to send a valid Hawk ticket. Do not use with the "auth" query string parameter.

      Query Parameters

      • auth: required (string)

        Used to send a valid Hawk ticket. Do not use with the "Authorization" header.

                Event Management

                Clusters are internal references for events or groups or teams, this collection aggregates the list of people and the video feeds used in a mission.

                Pre-plan Events

                Handles specific routes for event plans records

                Query Parameters


                accountDocId - get all event plans by account doc id

                status - get event plans by status Defaults to true



                /api/eventplans get post

                get

                CRUD calls for event plans

                post

                CRUD calls for event plans

                get /api/eventplans

                CRUD calls for event plans

                Secured by oz_ticket
                • Response
                • Security

                HTTP status code 200

                Body

                Media type: application/json

                Type: object

                Properties
                • planName: required (string - maxLength: 100)
                • createdBy: required (string)
                • accountDocId: (string)
                • address: (object)
                  • formattedAddress: (string - maxLength: 200)
                  • geo: (any)
                  • additionalInfo: (any)
                • description: (string)
                • feeds: (array of items)
                • isLocked: (boolean)
                • isShared: (boolean)
                • participants: (array of items)

                  Items: items

                  • participantDocId: required (string)
                  • role: required (string)
                  • status: required (boolean)
                • planId: (string)
                • status: (boolean)

                Example:

                {
  "accountDocId": "000000000000000000000002",
  "planName": "some name",
  "createdBy": "5c371aeab19f6b008411e880",
  "description": "some desc",
  "feeds": [
    "5c371aeab19f6b008411e880"
  ],
  "isLocked": false,
  "isShared": false,
  "participants": [
    {
      "participantDocId": "5c371aeab19f6b008411e880",
      "role": "2",
      "status": true
    }
  ],
  "planId": "some id",
  "status": true,
  "type": "some type"
}

                      /api/participants/doAuthenticate post

                      post

                      API to authenticate / let users login into STRAX

                      post /api/participants/doAuthenticate

                      API to authenticate / let users login into STRAX

                      • Request
                      • Response

                      Body

                      Media type: application/json

                      Type: object

                      Properties
                      • username: required (string - minLength: 3 - maxLength: 100 - pattern: [A-Z0-9a-z._+-@]*)

                        Valid email address provided by the agency

                        Example:

                        user@example.com
                      • password: required (string)

                        Example:

                        str*ngPa55w*rd
                      • fingerprint: (string)

                        A uniqe identifier for the device used to sign-in

                      • fpData: (array of )

                        List of parameters used to compute fingerprint

                      • applnType: required (one of Web Application, Android Application, iOS Application)

                        Type of application the user is logging in from

                      • applnName: required (one of STRAX APP AngularJS, STRAX APP VueJS, STRAX Mobile Android)

                      HTTP status code 200

                      Body

                      Media type: application/json

                      Type: object

                      Properties
                      • appTicket: required (object)

                        Application ticket used to request Auth ticket from ID Server. It contains the app-id and scope.

                        • firstName: required (string)
                        • lastName: required (string)
                        • partId: required (string)
                        • role: required (string)

                          As of now, role determines whether the user is a viewer, user, controller or EEI Support

                        • rsvp: required (string)

                          A string with grant associated to retrieve auth ticket from the ID server.

                        • token: required (string)

                          JWT token used to embed details required by the the UI

                        • vertical: (string)

                          LOB "eagleeye"

                        HTTP status code 401

                        Invalid Credentials

                        Body

                        Media type: application/json

                        Type: object

                        Properties
                        • code: required (string)
                        • message: required (string)

                        Example:

                        {
  "code": "STRLGN001",
  "message": "Invalid Credentials"
}

                        HTTP status code 500

                        Body

                        Media type: application/json

                        Type: object

                        Properties
                        • code: required (string)
                        • message: required (string)

                        Example:

                        {
  "code": "STRLGN004",
  "message": "Unable to login. System Error."
}

                        /api/preferences/{preferenceDocId} put get

                        put

                        This API sets the user preference for the device from which STRAX is accessed. Specify the device name for which the preference need to be set. Only the browser application will use preferenceDocId when the preference needs to be updated too many times for the same key. For eg., the FE app may need to set map preferences everytime it is moved.

                        /api/events/{clusterDocId}/participant/join post

                        post

                        Allow a participant to join this event by removing the participant from any other event. Since we display only the events assigned to for Users and Viewers, this API will just return the event response. Only for Controllers/Admin this API will remove teh user from other event and put them onto this before returning the event response.

                                  Used to send a valid Hawk ticket. Do not use with the "Authorization" header.

                                GIS Services to import ShapeFiles, KML & KMZ

                                Handles all Strax spefic GIS Services to import ShapeFiles, KML & KMZ

                                Query Parameters


                                Maplayers

                                status - boolean, used to get map layers by status


                                Maplayers/maplayerDocId

                                status - boolean, used to get map layers by status


                                Maplayers/maplayerDocId/features

                                bounds - string, Bounding rectangle(lat, lng, lat, lng) within which the map layer needs to be displayed separated by comma

                                Example 13.416633,144.7500333,12.500000,145.760000

                                subFeatureId - string, id of sub feature to search in features

                                                          STRAX Mile Stone REST

                                                          Handles all Strax spefic mile stone configuration and processing

                                                          Query Parameters


                                                          Not used in this API



                                                          MQTT Messages


                                                          Message indicating changing of camera position from cron task.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/milestone_service/angle-pan

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/milestone_service/angle-tilt

                                                          payload - { videoFeedId, degrees } , degress - from 0 to 360


                                                          Message indicating some one change PTZ of camera using API.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/milestone_service/ptz-change

                                                          payload - { videoFeedId }

                                                          /api/milestone/ptz post

                                                          Used for mile stone camera PTZ controls

                                                          post

                                                          Move camera in any direction

                                                          post /api/milestone/ptz

                                                          Move camera in any direction

                                                          Secured by oz_ticket
                                                          • Request
                                                          • Response
                                                          • Security

                                                          Body

                                                          Media type: application/json

                                                          Type: object

                                                          Properties
                                                          • _id: required (string)

                                                            Video feeds collection mongo Id

                                                          • pan: (integer)

                                                            Left and right moves. From -1 to 1. 1 = right, -1 = left.

                                                          • tilt: (integer)

                                                            Up and down moves. From -1 to 1. 1 = down, -1 = up.

                                                          • zoom: (integer)

                                                            Zoom in and out. From -1 to 1. 1 = zoom in, -1 = zoom out.

                                                          Example:

                                                          {
  "_id": "5bcf1cf0cd6a4fab5c7359b5",
  "pan": 1,
  "tilt": -1,
  "zoom": 0
}

                                                          /api/milestone/preset/{_id} get

                                                          get

                                                          Get preset information from camera by video feed mongo ID

                                                          get /api/milestone/preset/{_id}

                                                          Get preset information from camera by video feed mongo ID

                                                          Secured by oz_ticket
                                                          • Request
                                                          • Response
                                                          • Security

                                                          URI Parameters

                                                          • _id: required (string)

                                                          HTTP status code 200

                                                          Body

                                                          Media type: application/json

                                                          Type: object

                                                          Properties
                                                          • name: required (string)

                                                            Camera name

                                                          • ptzSettings: required (object)

                                                            Contains PTZ settings for camera

                                                            • ptzEnabled: required (boolean)
                                                          • presets: required (array of items)

                                                            Contains list of all presets in device

                                                            Items: items

                                                            • Id: required (string)

                                                              Id of preset in mile stone server

                                                            • Locked: required (string)

                                                              Defines if preset is locked

                                                            • Name: required (string)

                                                              Preset Name. Used in post call

                                                            • Position: required (object)

                                                              Preset PTZ position. Can be empty or NaN

                                                              • Pan: required (string)
                                                              • Tilt: required (string)
                                                              • Zoom: required (string)

                                                          Example:

                                                          {
  "name": "Camera name",
  "ptzSettings": {
    "ptzEnabled": true
  },
  "presets": [
    {
      "Id": "someId",
      "Locked": "false",
      "Name": "preset Name. Move_to_default",
      "Position": {
        "Pan": "NaN",
        "Tilt": "10",
        "Zoom": "4"
      }
    }
  ]
}

                                                          /api/milestone/monitoring/streams get

                                                          get

                                                          Wowza stream files monitoring statistic. Get information about every fixed stream

                                                          get /api/milestone/monitoring/streams

                                                          Wowza stream files monitoring statistic. Get information about every fixed stream

                                                          Secured by oz_ticket
                                                          • Response
                                                          • Security

                                                          HTTP status code 200

                                                          Body

                                                          Media type: application/json

                                                          Type: object

                                                          Properties
                                                          • wowza_stream_monitoring: required (array of items)

                                                            Wowza stream files statistic

                                                            Items: items

                                                            • stream_id: required (string)

                                                              id of stream

                                                            • connection_count: required (integer)

                                                              total connection to stream

                                                            • up_time: required (integer)

                                                              Up time in seconds(maybe milliseconds)

                                                            • response_code: required (integer)

                                                              http response code from wowza API call. 200 or 400 or 402 or 404 or 415

                                                            • error: required (integer)

                                                              0 - for success, 1 - for error

                                                            • error_message: required (string)

                                                              Empty for success, message for error

                                                          Example:

                                                          {
  "wowza_stream_monitoring": [
    {
      "stream_id": "new_stream",
      "connection_count": 22,
      "up_time": 71,
      "response_code": 200,
      "error": 1,
      "error_message": "Wowza API error message"
    }
  ]
}

                                                          STRAX trackers REST

                                                          Handles all Strax spefic tracker configuration and processing

                                                          Query Parameters


                                                          Trackers. Only for GET single tracker. GET /api/trackers/:ID

                                                          skip - hot many records to skip. By default return first 20. To get next 20 use skip=20

                                                          example - GET /api/trackers/:ID?skip=200



                                                          MQTT Messages


                                                          Message indicating new message in tracker.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/tracker_service/tracker/{trackerId}

                                                          payload - { _id, trackerDocId, messengerId, messengerName, unixTime, messageType, latitude, longitude, modelId, showCustomMsg, dateTime, messageDetail, batteryState, hidden, altitude }



                                                          /api/trackers get post

                                                          get

                                                          CRUD calls for trackers API

                                                          post

                                                          CRUD calls for trackers API

                                                          get /api/trackers

                                                          CRUD calls for trackers API

                                                          Secured by oz_ticket
                                                          • Response
                                                          • Security

                                                          HTTP status code 200

                                                          Body

                                                          Media type: application/json

                                                          Type: object

                                                          Properties
                                                          • name: required (string)
                                                          • type: (string - default: SPOT)

                                                            type of tracker

                                                          • baseUrl: required (string)

                                                            url where tracker can be requested

                                                          • trackerId: required (string)

                                                            tracker device id. Used to retrieve tracker data

                                                          • password: required (string)

                                                            password to get data from tracker used in pair with trackerId

                                                          • participantDocId: (string)

                                                            id of participant that enable tracker. On response returns participant info in object

                                                          • connected: (boolean - default: true)

                                                            is tracker connected

                                                          • battery: (string)

                                                            battery state

                                                          • status: required (boolean - default: true)

                                                            is tracker enabled.

                                                          • messages: (array of items)

                                                            Included in trackers GET response otherwise ignored. Last N tracker messages

                                                            Items: items

                                                            • _id: required (number)

                                                              message mongo _id

                                                            • altitude: required (number)
                                                            • batteryState: required (string)
                                                            • dateTime: required (datetime)

                                                              time in format YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS+0000

                                                            • hidden: required (number)
                                                            • latitude: required (number)
                                                            • longitude: required (number)
                                                            • messageDetail: required (string)
                                                            • messageType: required (string)
                                                            • messengerId: required (string)
                                                            • messengerName: required (string)
                                                            • modelId: required (string)
                                                            • showCustomMsg: required (string)
                                                            • unixTime: required (number)

                                                          Example:

                                                          {
  "name": "Tracker name",
  "type": "SPOT",
  "baseUrl": "someurl.trackers.com",
  "trackerId": "1x7qIQj33qBRQqJp2JL3JVEfWSfJlphzV",
  "password": "password",
  "participantDocId": "5ba29eb7dc77a5005c944347",
  "connected": false,
  "battery": "LOW",
  "status": true,
  "messages": [
    {
      "_id": 11111,
      "altitude": 33,
      "batteryState": "LOW",
      "dateTime": "2018-12-19T13:15:30.000Z",
      "hidden": 0,
      "latitude": 26.39722,
      "longitude": -80.09671,
      "messageDetail": "",
      "messageType": "UNLIMITED-TRACK",
      "messengerId": "0-3016697",
      "messengerName": "SHA-SPOT-Gen3",
      "modelId": "SPOT3",
      "showCustomMsg": "N",
      "unixTime": 1545225330
    }
  ]
}

                                                          delete /api/trackers/{_id}

                                                          CRUD calls for single tracker calls

                                                          Secured by oz_ticket
                                                          • Request
                                                          • Response
                                                          • Security

                                                          URI Parameters

                                                          • _id: required (string)

                                                          HTTP status code 200

                                                          Body

                                                          Media type: application/json

                                                          Type: object

                                                          Properties
                                                          • name: required (string)
                                                          • type: (string - default: SPOT)

                                                            type of tracker

                                                          • baseUrl: required (string)

                                                            url where tracker can be requested

                                                          • trackerId: required (string)

                                                            tracker device id. Used to retrieve tracker data

                                                          • password: required (string)

                                                            password to get data from tracker used in pair with trackerId

                                                          • participantDocId: (string)

                                                            id of participant that enable tracker. On response returns participant info in object

                                                          • connected: (boolean - default: true)

                                                            is tracker connected

                                                          • battery: (string)

                                                            battery state

                                                          • status: required (boolean - default: true)

                                                            is tracker enabled.

                                                          • messages: (array of items)

                                                            Included in trackers GET response otherwise ignored. Last N tracker messages

                                                            Items: items

                                                            • _id: required (number)

                                                              message mongo _id

                                                            • altitude: required (number)
                                                            • batteryState: required (string)
                                                            • dateTime: required (datetime)

                                                              time in format YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS+0000

                                                            • hidden: required (number)
                                                            • latitude: required (number)
                                                            • longitude: required (number)
                                                            • messageDetail: required (string)
                                                            • messageType: required (string)
                                                            • messengerId: required (string)
                                                            • messengerName: required (string)
                                                            • modelId: required (string)
                                                            • showCustomMsg: required (string)
                                                            • unixTime: required (number)

                                                          Example:

                                                          {
  "name": "Tracker name",
  "type": "SPOT",
  "baseUrl": "someurl.trackers.com",
  "trackerId": "1x7qIQj33qBRQqJp2JL3JVEfWSfJlphzV",
  "password": "password",
  "participantDocId": "5ba29eb7dc77a5005c944347",
  "connected": false,
  "battery": "LOW",
  "status": true,
  "messages": [
    {
      "_id": 11111,
      "altitude": 33,
      "batteryState": "LOW",
      "dateTime": "2018-12-19T13:15:30.000Z",
      "hidden": 0,
      "latitude": 26.39722,
      "longitude": -80.09671,
      "messageDetail": "",
      "messageType": "UNLIMITED-TRACK",
      "messengerId": "0-3016697",
      "messengerName": "SHA-SPOT-Gen3",
      "modelId": "SPOT3",
      "showCustomMsg": "N",
      "unixTime": 1545225330
    }
  ]
}

                                                          STRAX Media Service REST

                                                          Handles all Strax spefic video configuration and processing

                                                          Query Parameters


                                                          Flights

                                                          feedId - retrieve all the flights for a specific stream by its id

                                                          name - retrieve all the flights by the name of the stream

                                                          active - true to return all flights in flight - false to get completed flights

                                                          startRangeBegin - the first date in the range in querying when flights started

                                                          startRangeEnd - the last date in the range in querying when flights ended

                                                          endRangeBegin - the first date in the range in querying when flights ended

                                                          endRangeEnd - the last date in the range in querying when flights ended

                                                          status - true for unarchived, false for archived

                                                          corrdinates - retrieve all flights within this corrdinate range


                                                          Video Feeds

                                                          accout - retrieve all the feeds for a specific account

                                                          feedType - retrieve the feeds for a particular feed type such as uav or IPCamera

                                                          isAnalytic - true to return all feeds currently being used for analyitcs - false to return those that are not



                                                          MQTT Messages


                                                          Message indicating the starting and stopping of flights.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/flights/{feedId}

                                                          payload - action (start/stop),id (feedId), flightId, name (feed name), startTime


                                                          Message indicating the archiving and unarchiving of flights

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/flights/archive/{flightId}

                                                          payload - message (always equals refresh)


                                                          KLV message

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/klv/{feedId}

                                                          payload - timestamp,timeinmilli,headingAngle,pitchAngle,rollAngle,indicatedAirSpeed,designation, imageSourceSensor,sensorLatitude,sensorLongitude,altitude,horizontalField,verticalField, sensorAzimuthAngle,relativeElevationAngle,relativeRollAngle,slantRange,targetWidth, frameCenterLatitude,frameCenterLongitude,frameCenterElevation,offsetCornerLatitudePoint1, offsetCornerLongitudePoint1,offsetCornerLatitudePoint2,offsetCornerLongitudePoint2, offsetCornerLatitudePoint3,offsetCornerLongitudePoint3,offsetCornerLatitudePoint4, offsetCornerLongitudePoint4,windDirection,windSpeed,targetLocationLatitude, targetLocationLongitude,targetLocationElevation,targetErrorEstimateCE90, targetErrorEstimateLE90,groundSpeed,sensorNorthVelocity,sensorEastVelocity, feedId


                                                          This message sends the signal strength message for the video player.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/streams/throughput/{feedId}

                                                          payload - streamName, bar (value 0-4)


                                                          This message is used to control the red/green video icon

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/streams/message/{feedId}

                                                          payload - streamName, action (true of false)


                                                          This message is indicates a feed being added or remove from an event

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/streams/videofeeds{eventName}

                                                          payload - eventName, feedId, action (add or remove)


                                                          This message is sent when feed is added.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/videofeeds/create

                                                          payload - id,name,live,frameRate,capture,account,cameraType,feedType, klvUrl, wowzaUrl, isAnalytic


                                                          This message is sent when feed is updated.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/videofeeds/update

                                                          payload - id,name,live,frameRate,capture,account,cameraType,feedType, klvUrl, wowzaUrl, isAnalytic


                                                          This message is sent when feed is removed.

                                                          topic - 0/{account mneumonic}/media_service/videofeeds/remove

                                                          payload - id

                                                          /api/media/klv post

                                                          post

                                                          Post KLV for a UAV

                                                          post /api/media/klv

                                                          Post KLV for a UAV

                                                          Secured by oz_ticket
                                                          • Request
                                                          • Response
                                                          • Security

                                                          Body

                                                          Media type: application/json

                                                          Type: object

                                                          Properties
                                                          • eventType: required (string)

                                                            The event type

                                                          • deviceID: required (string)

                                                            The device id configured in UAV app - must equal name configured in Strax

                                                          • geoEvent: required (object)
                                                            • speed: required (number)

                                                              The speed the UAV is traveling at

                                                            • altitude: required (number)

                                                              The altitude the UAV is flying at

                                                            • bearing: required (number)

                                                              The direction the UAV is heading

                                                            • tlatitude: required (number)

                                                              The latitude of the target

                                                            • tlongitude: required (number)

                                                              The longitude of the target

                                                            • latitude: required (number)

                                                              The latitude of the UAV

                                                            • longitude: required (number)

                                                              The longitude of the UAV

                                                            • timestamp: required (number)

                                                              The timestamp of the record

                                                          Example:

                                                          {
  "eventType": "Telemetry Event",
  "deviceID": "testuav1",
  "geoEvent": {
    "speed": 44,
    "altitude": 500.3,
    "bearing": 77,
    "tlatitude": 27.40126,
    "tlongitude": -87.10857166666666,
    "latitude": 26.40126,
    "longitude": -80.10857166666666,
    "timestamp": 1481
  }
}
